  "python3 transform/ensembl/proteins.py"

dvc run --file outputs.ctrp.drugresponse.dvc --yes \
  -d source/ctrp/v20.meta.per_compound.txt \
  -d source/ctrp/v20.meta.per_cell_line.txt \
  -d source/ctrp/v20.data.curves_post_qc.txt \

  -d source/ctrp/v20.data.per_cpd_post_qc.txt \

  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.DrugResponse.Vertex.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.ResponseIn.Edge.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.ResponseTo.Edge.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.AliquotFor.Edge.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.Aliquot.Vertex.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.BiosampleFor.Edge.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.Biosample.Vertex.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.Individual.Vertex.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.InProject.Edge.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.Project.Vertex.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.InProgram.Edge.json.gz \
  -o outputs/ctrp/ctrp.Program.Vertex.json.gz \
  "python ./transform/ctrp/transform.py"
